<li>park, garden

***садить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:садить.html>сади́ть</a> (21636)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садить.html>сади́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sadítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посадить.html>посади́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to make or let someone sit down, to seat</li>
<li>to plant (e.g. trees or flowers)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to imprison, to put to jail</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:садить.html>сади́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:посадить.html>посади́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:засадить.html>засади́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-сад-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>.

***садиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:садиться.html>сади́ться</a> (879)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садить.html>сади́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садиться.html>сади́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sadítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сесть.html>сесть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sit down, to sit up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:садиться.html>сади́тесь</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:пожалуйста.html>пожа́луйста</a>.</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">formal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Sadítesʹ</b>, požálujsta.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Please <b>sit down</b>; please <b>get in/on</b> (e.g. a car)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take, to board, to get on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:садиться.html>сади́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:единица.html>едини́цу</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sadísʹ</b> na jedinícu</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>take</b> number one (tram, bus, etc.)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to sit down to</li>
<li>to land, to alight</li>
<li>to be imprisoned</li>
<li>to shrink (about clothes after washing)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садить.html>сади́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span> to</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The imperfective verb <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садиться.html>сади́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sadítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and its perfective counterpart <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сесть.html>сесть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are both intransitive despite the reflexive suffix <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> being absent in <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сесть.html>сесть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***саднить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:саднить.html>саднить</a> (21761)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sadьniti</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sadьno</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">садно́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sadnó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:саднить.html>са́днить</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:саднить.html>садни́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sádnitʹ</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sadnítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also  impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be sore <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from scrapes, abrasions, burns, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́гу</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:саднить.html>са́днит</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nógu <b>sádnit</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">my leg <b>is sore</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hurt (the heart, soul, etc.), to sadden, to cause emotional distress to</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> also  impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hurt <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in the heart, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to experience emotional distress
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдце</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:саднить.html>са́днит</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na sérdce <b>sádnit</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">my heart <b>hurts</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">са́днеть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sádnetʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">садно́</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sadnó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сад.html>са́д</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:нить.html>нить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сад.html>сад</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:нить.html>ни́ть</a></b>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сад.html>сад</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sad</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-óvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садовый.html>садо́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sadóvyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> garden; cultivated
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:садовый.html>садо́вая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:славка.html>сла́вка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sadóvaja</b> slávka</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>garden</b> warbler</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:садовый.html>садо́вый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шланг.html>шланг</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sadóvyj</b> šlang</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>garden</b> hose</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>са<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:выя.html>вы́й</a></b>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:производный.html>Произво́дное</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сад.html>сад</a></b> ➔ <a href = vnd.unilang:сад.html>сад</a> + <b>ов</b> + ый (суффиксальный).

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сад.html>сад</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sad</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fish pond <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">obsolete, dialectal, per Dal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садок.html>садо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sadók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садок.html>садка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садок.html>садки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садок.html>садко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fish pond <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">artificial pond for keeping and breeding fish</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>coop <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">room for keeping, breeding or fattening birds and small animals</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>name for a series of traps for animals and game</li></ol>

***сажать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сажать.html>сажа́ть</a> (4807)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сажать.html>сажа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sažátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посадить.html>посади́ть</a></b>)

<p><b>са<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жа́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сажень.html>сажень</a> (16402)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">сѧжень</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sęženĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sęženь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*se(n)g-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сажень.html>саже́нь</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сажень.html>са́жень</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sažénʹ</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sáženʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сажень.html>саже́ни</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сажень.html>са́жени</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сажень.html>саже́ни</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сажень.html>са́жени</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сажень.html>саже́ней</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сажень.html>сажене́й</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сажень.html>са́жен</a></b>)

<ol><li>sazhen, old Russian unit of length equal to 3 arshins or 2.134 meters or 7 feet</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:саквояж.html>саквоя́ж</a> (15152)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">sac de voyage</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:саквояж.html>саквоя́ж</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sakvojáž</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:саквояж.html>саквоя́жа</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:саквояж.html>саквоя́жи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:саквояж.html>саквоя́жей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>carpetbag (generally made from leather or heavy cloth)</li></ol>

<p><b>сак<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>я́ж</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сакраментальный.html>сакрамента́льный</a> (26547)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sacramentālis</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сакраментальный.html>сакрамента́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sakramentálʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сакрамента́льнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сакрамента́льней</b>)

<ol><li>sacramental</li>
<li>sacred, cherished</li>
<li>traditional, customary</li></ol>

***саксаул.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:саксаул.html>саксау́л</a> (27370)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kazakh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kazakh language">Kazakh</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="kk">сексеуіл</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="kk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">seksewil</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:саксаул.html>саксау́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">saksaúl</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:саксаул.html>саксау́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:саксаул.html>саксау́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:саксаул.html>саксау́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>saxaul <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">any of three species of the amaranth genus <i>Haloxylon</i></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:салага.html>сала́га</a> (17728)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:салага.html>сала́га</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">salága</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:салага.html>сала́ги</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:салага.html>сала́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:салага.html>сала́г</a></b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> noob, rookie, greenhorn (<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span>)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">noob</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сала́ка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">saláka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>са<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ла́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:га.html>га</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-салаг-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>
<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>О́бщее</a> прототипическое <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:мелкий.html>ме́лкая</a> пресноводная <a href = vnd.unilang:рыба.html>ры́ба</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:семейство.html>семе́йства</a> карповых, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:имеющий.html>име́ющая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:промысловый.html>промысло́вого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ния</a></i>.
</p>

***сало.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сало.html>са́ло</a> (4717)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:сало.html>са́ло</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">salo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sadlo</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сало.html>са́ло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sálo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сало.html>са́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сало.html>са́ла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сало.html>са́л</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>suet, fat, lard</li>
<li>tallow</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сальник.html>са́льник</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sálʹnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

Зализняка) |  <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> мн. ч. предположительны <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> неупотребимы.

***салон.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́н</a> (3787)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">salon</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">reception room</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">salón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>salon (fashionable shop or customer service), hairdressing salon
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́н</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:красота.html>красоты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>salón</b> krasoty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">beauty salon</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">массажный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">massažnyj <b>salón</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">massage parlour</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>show, exhibition
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авиационный.html>авиацио́нный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">aviaciónnyj <b>salón</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">air show</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:автомобильный.html>автомоби́льный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">avtomobílʹnyj <b>salón</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">motor show</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:демонстрационный.html>демонстрацио́нный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">demonstraciónnyj <b>salón</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">showroom</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>art gallery</li>
<li>lounge, waiting room
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́н</a></b> би́знес-кла́сса (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:аэропорт.html>аэропорту</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>salón</b> bíznes-klássa (v aeroportu)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">business/executive class lounge</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>cabin, passenger compartment
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́н</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:автомобиль.html>автомоби́ля</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>salón</b> avtomobílja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">inside of a car</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́н</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:класс.html>кла́сса</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> самолёте)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>salón</b> pérvovo klássa (v samoljóte)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">first class cabin/compartment</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>(reception with performing poets, musicians etc) salon</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> saloon</li></ol>
